   // Saddharmalaṅkāvatārasūtram //	// Sat Darma laFkA avatAra sUtram //
   om namo ratnatrayāya / om namaḥ sarvabuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ //	om namaH ratnatrayAya / om namaH sarva budDa boDisattveByaH //

   rāvaṇādhyeṣaṇāparivartaḥ prathamaḥ /	rAvaNa aDyezaNA parivartaH praTamaH /
   evaṃ mayā śrutam / ekasmin samaye bhagavāṃllaṅkāpure samudramalayaśikhare	evam mayA Srutam / ekasmin samaye BagavAn= laFkA pure samudra malaya SiKare
   viharati sma nānāratnagotrapuṣpapratimaṇḍite mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena sārdhaṃ	viharati sma nAnA ratna gotra puzpa pratimaNxite mahatA Bikzu saMGena sArDam
   mahatā ca bodhisattvagaṇena	mahatA ca boDisattva gaNena
   nānābuddhakṣetrasaṃnipatitairbodhisattvairmahāsattvaiḥ	nAnA budDa kzetra saMnipatitEH boDisattvEH mahAsattvEH
   anekasamādhivaśitābalābhijñāvikrīḍitairmahāmatibodhisattvapūrvaṃgamaiḥ	aneka samADi vaSitA bala aBijQA vikrIxitEH mahAm ati boDisattva pUrvaMgamEH

   pañcadharmasvabhāvavijñānanairātmyādvayagatiṃgataiḥ //	paQca Darma svaBAva vijQAna nErAtmya advaya gatiMgatEH //
   tena khalu punaḥ samayena bhagavān sāgaranāgarājabhavanāt saptāhenottīrṇa	tena Kalu punar samayena BagavAn sAgara nAga rAja BavanAt sapta ahena uttIrNa
   'bhūt / anekaśakrabrahmanāgakanyākoṭibhiḥ pratyudgamyamāno	aBUt / aneka Sakra brahma nAga kanyA kowiBiH pratyudgamyamAnaH 
   laṅkāmalayamavalokya smitamakarot   pūrvakairapi tathāgatairarhadbhiḥ	laFkA malayam avalokya smitam akarot  pUrvakEH api taTAgatEH arhadBiH
   samyaksaṃbuddhairasmiṃllaṅkāpurīmalayaśikhare	samyaksaMbudDEH asmin= laFkA purI malaya SiKare

   tadbhāvito dharmo deśitaḥ / yannvahamapi atraiva rāvaṇaṃ	tad BAvitaH DarmaH deSitaH / yat nu aham api atra eva rAvaNam
   yakṣādhipatimadhikṛtya etadevodbhāvayan dharmaṃ deśayeyam //	yakza aDipatim aDikRtya etat eva udBAvayan Darmam deSayeyam //
   aśrauṣīdrāvaṇo rākṣasādhipatistathāgatādhiṣṭhānāt   bhagavān kila	aSrOzIt rAvaNaH rAkzasa aDipatiH taTAgata aDizWAnAt  BagavAn kila
   sāgaranāgarājabhavanāduttīrya anekaśakrabrahmanāgakanyākoṭibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ	sAgara nAga rAja BavanAt uttIrya aneka Sakra brahma nAga kanyA kowiBiH parivRtaH
   puraskṛtaḥ samudrataraṃgānavalokya	puraskRtaH samudra taraMga an avalokya
   ālayavijñānodadhipravṛttivijñānapavanaviṣaye preritāṃstebhyaḥ	AlayavijQAna udaDi pravRtti vijQAna pavana vizaye preritAn= teByaH
   saṃnipatitebhyaścittānyavalokya tasminneva sthitaḥ udānamudānayati sma  	saMnipatiteByaH cittAni avalokya tasmin= eva sTitaH udAnam udAnayati sma  
   yannvahaṃ gatvā bhagavantamadhyeṣya laṅkāṃ praveśayeyam / tanme	yat nu aham gatvA Bagavantam aDyezya laFkAm praveSayeyam / tat me
   syāddīrgharātramarthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca //	syAt dIrGarAtram arTAya hitAya suKAya devAnAm ca manuzyANAm ca //
   atha rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipatiḥ saparivāraḥ pauṣpakaṃ vimānamadhiruhya yena	aTa rAvaNaH rAkzasa aDipatiH sa parivAraH pOzpakam vimAnam aDiruhya yena
   bhagavāṃstenopajagāma / upetya vimānādavatīrya saparivāro bhagavantaṃ	BagavAn= tena upajagAma / upetya vimAnAt avatIrya sa parivAraH Bagavantam
   triṣkṛtvaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tūryatālāvacaraiḥ pravādyadbhirindranīlamayena	trizkRtvas pradakziNIkRtya tUrya tAlA vacarEH pravAdyadBiH indranIla mayena
   daṇḍena vaiḍūryamusāra(galva)pratyuptāṃ vīṇāṃ priyaṅgupāṇḍunā anardhyeṇa	daNxena vExUrya musAra( galva) pratyuptAm vINAm priyaFgu pANxunA anarDyeNa
   vastreṇa pārśvāvalambitāṃ kṛtvā	vastreNa pArSva avalambitAm kRtvA
   ṣaḍjarṣabhagāndhāradhaivataniṣādamadhyamakaiśikagītasvaragrāmamūrchanādiyuktenānusārya	zaxja RzaBa gAnDAra DEvata nizAda maDyama kESika gIta svara grAma mUrCana Adi yuktena anusArya
   salīlaṃ vīṇāmanupraviśya gāthābhigītairanugāyati sma  	sa lIlam vINAm anupraviSya gATA aBigItEH anugAyati sma

   pratyātmavedyagatisūcanakaṃ deśehi nāyaka iha dharmanayam // Lank_1.1 //	pratyAtma vedya gati sUcanakam deSehi nAyakaH iha Darmanayam // Lank _1.1 //
   (Vaidya 2)	(VEdyaH 2)
   śubhadharmasaṃcitatanuṃ sugataṃ nirmāṇanirmitapradarśanakam /	SuBa Darma saMcita tanum sugatam nirmANa nirmita pradarSanakam /

   laṅkāmimāṃ pūrvajinādhyuṣitāṃ putraiśca teṣāṃ bahurūpadharaiḥ /	laFkAm imAm pUrva jina aDyuzitAm putrEH ca tezAm bahu rUpa DarEH /
   deśehi nātha iha dharmavaraṃ śroṣyanti yakṣa bahurūpadharāḥ // Lank_1.3 //	deSehi nATaH iha Darma varam Srozyanti yakza bahu rUpa DarAH // Lank _1.3 //
   atha rāvaṇo laṅkādhipatiḥ toṭakavṛttenānugāyya punarapi	aTa rAvaNaH laFkA aDipatiH towaka vRttena anugAyya punar api
   gāthābhigītenānugāyati sma  	gATA aBigItena anugAyati sma

   sthitamātrasya buddhasya rāvaṇo hyapsaraiḥ saha /	sTita mAtrasya budDasya rAvaNaH hi apsarEH saha /
   yakṣaiśca nānāvividhaiḥ śukasāraṇapaṇḍitaiḥ // Lank_1.5 //	yakzEH ca nAnA viviDEH Suka sAraNa paNxitEH // Lank _1.5 //
   ṛddhyā gatvā tamadhvānaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati nāyakaḥ /	RdDyA gatvA tam aDvAnam yatra tizWati nAyakaH /

   rāvaṇo 'haṃ daśagrīvo rākṣasendra ihāgataḥ /	rAvaNaH aham daSagrIvaH rAkzasa indraH iha AgataH /

   pūrvairapi hi saṃbuddhaiḥ pratyātmagatigocaram /	pUrvEH api hi saMbudDEH pratyAtma gati gocaram /

   deśanānayanirmuktaṃ pratyātmagatigocaram /	deSanA naya nirmuktam pratyAtma gati gocaram /

   (Vaidya 3)	(VEdyaH 3)
   yakṣiṇyo yakṣaputrāśca mahāyānabubhutsavaḥ /	yakziNyaH yakza putrAH ca mahAyAna buButsavaH /

   ārūḍhaḥ puṣpake yāne rāvaṇenopanāmite // Lank_1.23 //	ArUXaH puzpake yAne rAvaNena upanAmite // Lank _1.23 //

   apsarairhāsyalāsādyaiḥ pūjyamānāḥ purīṃ gatāḥ // Lank_1.24 //	apsarEH hAsya lAsa AdyEH pUjyamAnAH purIm gatAH // Lank _1.24 //

   (Vaidya 4)	(VEdyaH 4)

   atha vā dharmatā hyeṣā dharmāṇāṃ cittagocare /	aTa vA DarmatA hi ezA DarmANAm citta gocare /
   na ca bālāvabudhyante mohitā viśvakalpanaiḥ // Lank_1.41 //	na ca bAla avabuDyante mohitAH viSva kalpanEH // Lank _1.41 //
   na draṣṭā na ca draṣṭavyaṃ na vācyo nāpi vācakaḥ /	na drazwA na ca drazwavyam na vAcyaH na api vAcakaH /

   (Vaidya 5)	(VEdyaH 5)
